  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_c652520b-8083-40e7-b9e2-1a4436f6fd39'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText11372153044006332269" style="display:none">A male prostitute, a mangy cat, a murder and a maniacal mix-up that threatens his career, his impending marriage and his life. Nothing is going as planned for Austin Glass.<br /><br />Austin—seems to have it all. At least on the surface. A loving fiancee. A future with the FBI and a healthy sized trust fund. He also has a grin and a wisecrack for every situation. But the smile he presents to everyone hides a painful past he’s buried too deeply to remember. And his quips mask bitterness and insecurity. Austin has himself and most of the whole world fooled. Until he meets someone who immediately sees him better than he sees himself.<br /><br />As events unfold and Austin’s world unravels, he finds himself pushed into making quick life-changing decisions. But can he trust Peter or what’s happening between them when each meeting seems to be just a series of volatile reactions?</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer404555180" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15400233048656813719"><b>“I'm not gay.” That wasn't what I meant to say.<br/>“Congratulations. Would you like a medal?” Bunny Slippers asked.<br/>“I already have a medal. For bravery, not for being gay. I think you made me gay.”<br/>“I made you gay?” He set down the napkin he was holding. “Is that better or worse than the person who made you stupid?”</b><br/><br/><a target='_blank' title='ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting' href='http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/11/tumblrmaplzdj0eq1rc77er.jpg/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389682i/750931.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><b>This book doesn't have enough pages. <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=279453.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/360663.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a> <br/>There is one chapter here named "Never ending story". THAT'S what this book should have been! <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=279453.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/360663.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/>I just wanted to read it, and read it, and read it, </b></span>
  <span id="freeText15400233048656813719" style="display:none"><b>“I'm not gay.” That wasn't what I meant to say.<br>“Congratulations. Would you like a medal?” Bunny Slippers asked.<br>“I already have a medal. For bravery, not for being gay. I think you made me gay.”<br>“I made you gay?” He set down the napkin he was holding. “Is that better or worse than the person who made you stupid?”</b><br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/11/tumblrmaplzdj0eq1rc77er.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389682i/750931.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>This book doesn't have enough pages. <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=279453.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/360663.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <br>There is one chapter here named "Never ending story". THAT'S what this book should have been! <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=279453.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/360663.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>I just wanted to read it, and read it, and read it, didn't really care if that meant too many stories for the characters, I'd read it if they'd suddenly decided to move on Mars and catch aliens! <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=27545.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374085ra/727998.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>The writing is simply brilliant! And just for that this book deserves 5 stars. The characters and the story - fantastic! Loved them both, and loved the story, every second of it. I didn't want it to end (well I said that already, sorry <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=54273.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/352106.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> ).</b><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“People aren't always who they seem, Detective. Am I anything like you thought?”<br>“No,” I admitted. <i>You're a million times better than I could have imagined</i>. And that was the problem. Looking at Peter, I realized that I was never going to get over him. A distressing thought when I considered I might not ever <i>have</i> Peter.</b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>The story</b><br><br>One day, while sitting at a diner, Austin notices a pair of bunny slippers. Then he notices the guy wearing them. Then he notices his face, his eyes, his hair, his body, his lips, and again, his freaking bunny slippers. And THEN he thinks he just might be gay. But that's impossible, right? You don't suddenly turn gay at age 26 at the sight of some bunny slippers and a freakishly gorgeous guy wearing them, right? <b>RIGHT?</b> Hmm. Well, of course, the logical explanation would be that he has a bunny-slipper sexual fetish, or that the guy is responsible for turning him gay all of the sudden <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=703126.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/363966.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>That was the birth of an obsession, well, two actually, one for the slippers, one for the guy <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=767622.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222758i/362324.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>What didn't help with his messed up love life was having a fiance, and working on a case that's directly involved with Mr. Bunny Slippers' family and former lover <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=963779.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374025ra/727914.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Besides, for our date Saturday? I was thinking less cell block and more movie house.” I said brightly.<br>His lips twitched, but he didn't say no. I took that as ‘Oh, you sexy devil, Austin, I want to do you right here, but I'm super-duper excited about our date so I'll wait’.<br>I was paraphrasing, of course.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>Austin</b><br><br>I love that guy :D He's so messed up <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=703126.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/363966.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>He's working for the police, but aiming for the FBI. He's very intelligent, doesn't do lying, he says the first things that pop up to his mind, and is very good at reading people.<br>After meeting Bunny Slippers, he can't get him out of his head, so he begins to question his sexuality. That leads to some dark memories (oh that was just terrible, Jesse and all <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=468813.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/374889.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> ) and him finally realising who he is.<br>He has such a funny mind and I loved his inner monologue :D<br>The scenes with Peter :D excellent :) Even though, most of the time he doesn't even know what to do with him, they both send mixed signals, they're both messed up and complicated, and they both don't want to fall in love, but of course...<br>My fav scene with him was when he was trying to wash Peter's hands and Peter kept trying to tell him he was clean. Heart. Broke. Mine. Totally. <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=468813.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/374889.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I think he finally realised that Peter was more than a whore and that he kept saying it just to put a distance between them. <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=4197637437.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/354124.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Oh and another one, when he kept telling Peter to ask him for money. <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=815594.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/348723.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Rabbit's the rock we cling to when we're drowning. He needs a mountain to hold him up, not another storm that'll wear away at him.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>Bunny Slippers/Peter</b><br><br>Taken from the streets and adopted by a former cop, Peter is now the owner of the diner Austin keeps stalking. For years now, he's been taking care of Cai and Darryl, the other two kids the cop adopted, and they've had a tough life, mostly Peter and Darryl working as prostitutes to get the meds for Cai, who's bipolar. He doesn't know what Austin wants with him, and thinks that he, like everyone else before him, only sees his looks, wants fim for nothing but sex. So he propositions himself, and Austin, obsessed as he is, accepts <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=798186.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222758i/362515.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> Won't say how it all ended :P but let's just say it led to their first date <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=biggestgrin_zps92d5aecd.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/372503.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Peter... Even though he's so young (20), he's too mature for his age, and I can believe it because of the life he had. He is basically more mature than Austin, at least that's how I saw them. They fit each other perfectly. The impossible couple, a cop and a prostitute <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=1059282649.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380372925ra/726346.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I felt really bad for him, but loved him all the more for his devotion to Cai and Darryl, he took care of them for a long time, and would do anything to protect them, even lie to the cops (Austin) regarding the case and a murder Cai could be involved in.<br><br><br><br>This is Darryl's rant about Austin and Peter fighting XD one of my favorite quotes hahahah :D<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I love you. No you don't. I don't love you. Yes you do. Wah wah wah. Some of us wanted to sleep!”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Here's Austin's rant after a fight with Peter XD<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>And damn Peter, too, while I was at it. And his fucking bunny slippers that made me interested enough to pay attention to him in the first place. I was burning those fuzzy fuckers the moment I saw them again.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><b>Well, this book had it all <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=356261_zps88c12ca1.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380372925ra/726348.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>Amazing writing, humor, excellent characters, great story, romance, action, angst, hot sexy times, and a beautiful happy ending <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=836920.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/356484.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>What more could I ask for? <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=836920.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/356484.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br>Oh wait! I could ask more! <br><br><br>More books! Now! I can't wait to read Cai's story <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=1839924927.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/365269.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> </b><br><br><br><br></span>

Give him my best please. I do hope he'll continue to write such compelling and entertaining stories in the future.</s><br/><br/>I've been in a very serious book slump for a rather long time and decided to do a re-read of your fantabulous story Shattered Glass. Guess wh</span>
  <span id="freeText8349904485627448002" style="display:none"><b>5 stars. Re-read 09/14. Review edited September 29, 2014.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411898412i/11297023.jpg" alt=" photo oie_m9NaUIUAV8tY_zpsbdf29ba2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411925654ra/11300780.gif" alt=" photo oie_pNSPFbRkIifG_zps203ef1a8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dear Austin,<br><br><s>I've read your story <i>Shattered Glass.</i> Well, I wanted to know what the fuss is all about, and…<b>holy cow, was I ever impressed!</b> Dani Alexander has written an amazingly good book. Give him my best please. I do hope he'll continue to write such compelling and entertaining stories in the future.</s><br><br>I've been in a very serious book slump for a rather long time and decided to do a re-read of your fantabulous story Shattered Glass. Guess what? I'm back in my happy place and wanted to quote the whole darn book! I feel so crazy good. Fantastic. Awesome. Yes, yes, yes! *high fives* I'm sorry for my little outburst. *sheepish smile* I'll be back to acting demurely stat.<br><br>Okey-dokey, let's get down to business, my dear. What the heck is wrong with you? I mean do you really have a bunny slipper fetish and not a c*ck sucking fixation? Think it over. My best guess is you're addicted to both. Do you remember when your fantasies were filling with images of Peter's mouth on naked things of yours? You were thinking about naked things with a <i>guy.</i> It was pretty surreal, wasn't it? Of course at that time you were so not gay. After all, you don't go twenty-six years before the gay gene suddenly just kicks in. As if. Austin, my dear, you were in complete denial.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411898412ra/11297025.gif" alt=" photo oie_AYSDJS6Ex9Bh_zps4e5c0a3e.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411898412i/11297026.png" alt=" photo oie_lWNzNFuQtdD0_zps1a7361b1.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411898412ra/11297027.gif" alt=" photo oie_GsEQpA3a1Y7U_zpsf267f671.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let's talk about Peter now. I didn't particularly like him in the beginning of your story. Although the more I read he somehow grew on me and, in the end, I even fell for him. Besides, all that matters is that you love him. When you're happy then I'm happy, too. You didn't want him to waste his life busing tables. You were obsessed with his freckles, his bunny slippers and his lips. Yeah, Peter was a witness and possible person of interest and you were dating him, <i>a whore, *gasp*</i> while working on the vice squad. I'd say that's a pretty bad call. But then again, Peter made you incredibly horny all.The.F*cking.Time. Eventually you got it that Peter wasn't a whore anymore. Oh, and let's not forget your fiancée, Angelica, who didn't want to talk to you anymore. It was kinda understandable, wasn't it? Dear Peter is playing you like the Philharmonic's conductor and he alternated between being hostile, affectionate, murderous, manipulative and horny. Let's not forget the <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[death kid <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> either. He made you think. When you slowly peeled your life apart, it really helped you to realize how lonely and afraid <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Jesse <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> must have been. A dawning of understanding washed over you. It sure as heck was a real eye-opener to you. Peter was the <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Jesse <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> that could have been and some little piece of you believed the universe gave you a do-over. Thus, was I ever glad when you recognized and accepted your sexual orientation. Finally you were fully embracing the gay in all its glory.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411898412ra/11297028.gif" alt=" photo oie_io1gCH6NwPuJ_zpsd4a609e7.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"You want to have sex in a men's bathroom?"<br>"Huh? You said…Wasn't it a signal? Your coming in here? I read online that gay men did that."<br>"Yah, int he 1960's, Austin. Or at a Republican National Convention. Not on the first date in the bathroom of a restaurant. In this century.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411898412ra/11297029.gif" alt=" photo oie_s3RhIdS90Cuz_zpsc2154d77.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Good?" Peter laughed, placing his hands on the floor at either side of my hips and leaning forward to my ear. "Hope you took notes. There will be an oral quiz later."<br>"Notes? Fuck. I don't think I could repeat that if I had a video and step-by-step instructions."<br>Video…mm.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411898412i/11297024.png" alt=" photo oie_7IsXb5hV2X8P_zps515e421b.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Although you still believed that you were unlovable. Austin, you are so f*cked up, and Peter was going to break you. That said, this special moment did come and finally you broke. It wasn't a visible fracture, and you didn't sob or explode into anguish. You didn't give in to your vomitus urge that came from the burst of self-loathing either. Yet you just shattered nonetheless.<br><br>Your father and mother are hypocritical, abandoning, and homophobic assholes. Gah. You cracked me up, Austin, when you told your father about your <i>ho-mo-seckshuul</i> boyfriend. OMG, Austin Glass the <i>Homo-extraordinaire Strikes Again!</i> By the way, I loved your favorite term <i>Butt Pirate.</i><br><br>I really adored Angelica, your fiancée. Oops, I'm sorry, ex-fiancée. She's a very kind and uncomplicated woman. Even though you hurt her by being gay, she took it in stride eventually. I know you are grateful to have such a wonderful and understanding friend.<br><br>Fact is, the cast of secondary characters is interesting and really great. Granted, I'm not very fond of Darryl, the prick, even though I enjoyed his bold mouth. <i>Eeny meeny miney homo…</i><br><br>Of course I liked Luis, your partner:<br><br><b>
  <i>"I said I'd had enough of this shit, you stupid stubborn ass."<br>"I love you, too. Which is why I say this with respect: If you keep rubbing your face like that, I'm going to have to lift up skin to look you in the eyes."<br><br>*******<br>I had to grin, desperate though it was.<br>"Kiss it and make it all better, daddy?"<br>"Tell me again why I put up with you?"<br>"I always let you drive?"<br>"That's so you can stare at my cock."<br>"I hear gay men are allergic to polyester and bad fashion. Your cock will always be safe."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411898412ra/11297030.gif" alt=" photo oie_Xr61AIsGTYvx_zpsaf984d1f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I liked the bipolar and hypomanic Cai. I'm not sure yet if I'll be joining the <i>Cult of Cai,</i> though. Besides, I don't think he's the next coming of Christ either. On the other hand, I have to admit that Cai is a very special and complex person. You know I think that Riley is super-duper sexy and the age difference between these two guys does intrigue me all the more. <br><br>I laughed my ass off when you found this strange creature called cat.<br><br><b>
  <i>The cat? Looked maimed, or burned. Her random tufts of fur were indiscriminately stuck between bits of pink skin. It was like a four-year-old had used dust bunnies from under the bed to create a collage of fur on a burlap canvas. The cat reeked. The thing was a walking biohazard of stale tuna seeped in sun-soured milk.<br>(…)<br>"I've been at homicide scenes that smelled better than you," I told it.<br>Purr.<br>"Dogs are okay, but I don't like cats."<br>Blink.<br>Do you know why I like dogs and not cats? Because when you're talking to dogs, they don't walk away in order to rim themselves."<br>(…)<br>With a sigh, I returned the notebook to the shelf and gave the masturbating cat a grimace.<br>"You're like a self-published pet porno." It ignored me. "I don't want to see this again," I warned it, flapping a hand at the self-gratification show.</i>
</b><br><br>Austin, could you do me a favor? Do tell Dani that I loved Shattered Glass. I really dig his writing. It felt like a breath of fresh air and I had so much fun devouring your entertaining story. Dani’s writing is full of passion, that’s for sure, and I think he’s a man who loves to laugh because I really liked to indulge in his well-placed humor. Having said that, I’m pretty sure that Dani doesn’t take himself too seriously either. As it was, your story provided so many heartfelt laughs. I love it when a book can make me smile again and again and yet at the same time I really dug the emotional and sad moments, too. Do you want to know what else I did like? I adored the well-drawn and complex characters, the fantastic and hilarious dialogue, and the crazy-good plot. Boy, there was so much stuff going on here! Also, there were some nice twists that I didn’t see coming, and last but not least I really liked the hot and intimate smexy times. Austin, I hope you do appreciate it that I can’t think of anything that I disliked. I assure you that’s no mean feat because the more books I read the more critical I become. For once no lamenting at all. Be happy!<br> <br>Take care and all the best,<br> <br>Baba<br> <br> <br> <br>P.S. Tell Cai that I’m looking forward to reading his story. It's a long wait but we all know that good things come to those who wait.<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer110791255335936904"><br/><b>***I LOVED THIS BOOK EVEN MORE THE SECOND TIME!!!***</b> May 2013<br/><br/>I just LOVED it, I can put into words what I feel for Peter *SIGH*. I just need <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13420353.Not_So_Innocent__Shattered_Glass___2_' title='Not So Innocent (Shattered Glass, #2) by Dani Alexander' rel='nofollow noopener'>Not So Innocent</a> like NOW!<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408344i/798758.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Thanks Ladies for this great BR. I am sooooo glad you popped your cherry with this one! </b><br/><br/>---------PREVIOUS REVIEW------------- Feb 2013<br/><br/><b>FIVE HILARIOUS & HOT STARS!!!<br/><br/>I loved this book!!!</b><br/><br/>This is the story about Austin & Peter, aka Rabbit.<br/><br/><b>***AUSTIN***</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408344i/798759._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b> "Tell me something good about your life"</b><br/><br/><b>***PETER, AKA RABBIT***</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379785632i/472733.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b> "You" </b><br/><br/>Austin is work</span>
  <span id="freeText110791255335936904" style="display:none"><br><b>***I LOVED THIS BOOK EVEN MORE THE SECOND TIME!!!***</b> May 2013<br><br>I just LOVED it, I can put into words what I feel for Peter *SIGH*. I just need <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13420353.Not_So_Innocent__Shattered_Glass___2_" title="Not So Innocent (Shattered Glass, #2) by Dani Alexander" rel="nofollow noopener">Not So Innocent</a> like NOW!<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408344i/798758.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Thanks Ladies for this great BR. I am sooooo glad you popped your cherry with this one! </b><br><br>---------PREVIOUS REVIEW------------- Feb 2013<br><br><b>FIVE HILARIOUS &amp; HOT STARS!!!<br><br>I loved this book!!!</b><br><br>This is the story about Austin &amp; Peter, aka Rabbit.<br><br><b>***AUSTIN***</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408344i/798759._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b> "Tell me something good about your life"</b><br><br><b>***PETER, AKA RABBIT***</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379785632i/472733.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b> "You" </b><br><br>Austin is working for the FBI, he is about to get married and has a “perfect” life. Enter Peter, aka Rabbit (aka Bunny Slippers). He is the hottest red haired guy ever with the most beautiful blue eyes in the world. What, you don’t trust me? Ok, let Austin explain how blue Peter’s eyes are:<br><br><b> Blue eyes. No, not just blue, blue like glacial waters, like romantic poems, like heavens and moonstones. Cornflower blue. And-<br><i>Blue like romantic poems? </i> What the ever-living fuck? </b><br><br>Well, as you can imagine, after their first encounter Austin reconsiders his sexuality but he is sure that he is NOT gay. First, because he was engaged to a woman. Second, because he masturbated to images of women. Third, because people don’t wake up gay… and a lot of more stupid reasons…<br><br>So what is the best idea he has? Yes, he goes to talk to Peter and tell him he is NOT gay. OMG! Austin seriously needs help! LOL<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408344i/798760.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>”I am not gay”<br>“Congratulations, would you like a medal?”<br>“I already have a medal. For bravery, not for being gay. I think you made me gay.”<br>“I made you gay? Is that better or worse than the person who made you stupid?” </b><br><br>At this point I must say <b> I love reading about people discovering their sexuality </b>, I am kinda tired of people saying ‘hey, he is 20, he should have realized before’. Come on! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ go fuck yourselves <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Austin has a hard time accepting he is gay so he decides to call his sexuality <b>”bunny-slipper-sexual”</b><br><br>I loved the way Austin was totally attracted to Peter, like he could not stop thinking about him all day long. *SIGH*<br><br><b>”I like you. Even though you’re probably a criminal and are going to get me thrown off the force. And you kicked me. Broke my nose. Made me gay and refuse to kiss me” </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408344ra/798761.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really want to quote the whole damn book because I bookmarked almost every single page! I mean, this is a perfectly written book, I loved loved loved all smart ass comments, it was HILARIOUS, SUPER DIVERTIDO!<br>And yes, I agree with Austin, Thursdays suck BIG TIME!<br><br><i>Thursdays are that awful place between halfway done and can’t quite see the finish line yet</i><br><br>Days go by and Austin’s feelings get stronger because even though Peter looks like a criminal (or at least his family is) he is also a very special guy who takes care of his family. He is not selfish, he never asks for anything for him, they only thing he wants is protecting his family, specially his brothers Cai &amp; Darryl.<br><br><b>”Tell me something good about your life”<br>“You”</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408344i/798762.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Austin realizes Peter is really a good guy and decides to help him no matter what, even if he loses his job… <br><br><b>Even the road to Disneyland has potholes<br>“Money is why I do that. Cai is why I breathe” </b><br><br>Austin &amp; Luis, his co-worker, are investigating a human trafficking operation and Peter is involved in the story so Austin has a hard time to decide if he should be professional or if he should follow his instincts and support Peter and his family (and animals lol).<br><br>At the same time he has to deal with his father, who obviously won’t accept him being gay (which is not a problem because Austin doesn’t care).<br><br>Funny thing is his father and his ex-fiancee will end up helping Peter and his brothers to prove their innocence. <br><br>I don’t really want to spoil their love story and the investigation but I want everyone to read this AH-MAZING &amp; hilarious book, I loved loved loved it! Come on guys, give it a try ;)<br><br><b>”You don’t even know me”<br>“Which makes it really weird to be falling for you, don’t you think?” </b><br><br>Some of the best quotes on the second half of the book:<br><br>*My brilliance could be measured in milligrams<br><br>*I’d had better delivered kisses, but the Fourth of July had fewer fireworks than this one<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/459789.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*Gay sex, one. Straight sex, zero.<br><br>*”I prefer you overall”<br>*”It’s a pull out, you two can share”. <i> Over my dead, rotted-to-dust corpse! <br><br>*”Your father also killed and maimed people for a living. <b>How about we just place him in the Not-To-Emulate pile?</b>”<br><br>*”Your decorator? Seriously? <b>How did you not know you were gay?</b>”<br>*<b><i> You’ve already ruined your career, your marriage, possibly your partnership, definitely your reputation, and most likely your house. Are you really going to draw the line at taking a cat home? </i> </b><br><br>*”I liked it when you called it home” GOOSEBUMPS!<br><br>*<b>”And if your ass didn’t hurt I’d fuck you so hard into the mattress you’d forget every word except ‘more’ and ‘please’!”</b><br><br>*”<i>Sucking</i> in bed is probably why he’s changing teams”.<br><br>*<b>”Am I anything like you thought?”<br>“No”. <i>You’re a million times better than I could have imagined</i> </b><br><br>*”Rabbit’s the rock we cling to when we’re drowning. He needs a mountain to hold him up, not another storm that’ll wear away at him”<br><br>*”I love you. No you don’t. I don’t love you. Yes you do. Wah wah wah”<br><br>*”Ask him something useful. Like does he love me not?”<br><br>*“Do you know what I did to the last guy that called me Tinkerbelle?"<br>"Slept with him?"<br>Darryl was silent for a second. "After that.”<br><br>*"Hard-ons don't make you think less. They make you think stupid. Which makes me think you must have one 24/7.”<br><br>*“I looked at our hands, caked and coated in red, but entwined. The pristine moment when they were clasped like that earlier in the day seemed weeks ago.<br>"Clean." Peter said.<br>"Can I get a water bottle or something to clean his hands?" <br>"No. I'm...clean."<br><b>I had missed who Peter was until that very moment.<br>I had called him names and treated him callously. I had read every micro expression in a vacuum of how it related to Austin Glass. And in return Peter had cared for my wounds, treated me tenderly and assured me that he was HIV negative while bleeding out in a hallway of strangers </b><br><br>*“Then I guess the rest of my life will be resigned to doggy style sex."<br><br>*<b>”I already found out that marriage isn’t what holds people together, Austin. And infidelity isn’t what tears them apart.”</b> TRUE STORY!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408344ra/798763.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>***BUDDY READ WITH LACI, RATCH, RAIN, RENEE &amp; SHELLY***<br><br>***Forgot to mention, this is the first chapter of Cai's book. My lovely LACI sent me the link yesterday***</b><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://slashfiction.org/not-so-innocent/">http://slashfiction.org/not-so-innocent/</a></i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_323376717" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/323376717" />
    <a title="Monique" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6875778-monique"><img alt="Monique" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1584362433p2/6875778.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/323376717?book_show_action=true">May 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Monique" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Monique" href="/user/show/6875778-monique">Monique</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6875778-monique?shelf=all-time-favourites">all-time-favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6875778-monique?shelf=lgbt">lgbt</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer323376717" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12863010271249299225"><b>The writing is brilliant. The story riveting. The characters captivating.. What we are blessed with is a truly wonderful novel and a sheer delight to read ~ no matter the cost, this book is a gift and I thank you Dani Alexander for sharing it with us...</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1166.photobucket.com/albums/q618/Monique_Lehane/?action=view&current=tumblr_lsnb2bgT0E1qmz21po1_500-1.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380376771i/731844.jpg' alt='tumblr_lsnb2bgT0E1qmz21po1_500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This is the funniest book I have read this year, (crying laughing and totally in love with Austin) Your humour Dani is so seamlessly woven throughout the fabric of the book - and incorporates the romance and the crime thriller combined. This i</span>
  <span id="freeText12863010271249299225" style="display:none"><b>The writing is brilliant. The story riveting. The characters captivating.. What we are blessed with is a truly wonderful novel and a sheer delight to read ~ no matter the cost, this book is a gift and I thank you Dani Alexander for sharing it with us...</b><br><br><a href="http://s1166.photobucket.com/albums/q618/Monique_Lehane/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_lsnb2bgT0E1qmz21po1_500-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380376771i/731844.jpg" alt="tumblr_lsnb2bgT0E1qmz21po1_500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is the funniest book I have read this year, (crying laughing and totally in love with Austin) Your humour Dani is so seamlessly woven throughout the fabric of the book - and incorporates the romance and the crime thriller combined. This isn't a romance with a little action, or a thriller with a sprinkling of passion... it is simply the whole package, perfectly put together, with an epilogue that leaves us salivating for the next instalment... *wink* *wink*<br><br>My review would never do justice to this book, it really is one of those you have to read to experience, to understand what a truly fabulous read it is. A friend of mine recently accused me of writing novella length reviews - If I put into words the wonders contained within, never mind the copious amounts of quotes I highlighted... this would be novel length! So I will endeavour to keep it short!!<br><br>We meet Austin in a dingy dinner... Dazed and in a trance, totally captivated by the vision before him, like a diamond in the sky this boy before him shone so bright he was transfixed by his beauty.<br><br><blockquote>
<i>"Blue eyes. No, not just blue, blue like glacial waters, like poems, like heavens and moonstones. Cornflower blue. And...</i><br><br>Blue like romantic poems? What the ever-living fuck?</blockquote><br><br>Model beautiful, thick red hair and freckles, lots of piercing's, tattoos... Oh, and not forgetting the blue eyes!! This was the bus boy - and he was wearing bunny slippers!?!<br><br><a href="http://s1166.photobucket.com/albums/q618/Monique_Lehane/?action=view&amp;current=apair.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380376771ra/731845.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Austin doesn't know this boy, has never seen him before... he is confused, perplexed and having a major identity crisis! He couldn't understand <i>how</i> he could be having sexual thoughts and feelings for a MAN!... after all "he was NOT gay" So Austin does the only sensible thing he could think of - he ask's his friends!?! Then comes to the the <i>lightbulb</i> conclusion that it really isn't his fault... Oh no. It was Bunny slippers - he <i>made</i> him gay... there was no other explanation!?! <br><br>Austin Glass is outrageously honest, to the point where most would think he is either joking or very rude, when in fact, he is just speaking his mind!... it's as though the words come tumbling out before his brain engages and there is a child like innocence behind his reasoning! His life is a dilemma... and like a petulant child he needs attention and he will stamp his feet 'till he gets it! Austin may be 26 years old but... he has the mental age of a hormonal teenager! Selfish in his opinions and no diplomacy skills WHATSOEVER!<br><br>In the middle of all the shenanigans with Bunny slippers, Austin is investigating a human trafficking operation. So when the object of his obsession is thrown into the frame... his emotions are torn between trust and accusation and tossed back and forth between hope and despair!<br><br>Bunny Slippers, does have a name... Peter Cotton or Rabbit as he is affectionately know as by his brothers Cai and Darryl. They are his life and reason for living, their welfare is paramount - especially Cai, who at 16 suffers from bipolar and depends on both Peter and Darryl, who in turn prostitute themselves to care for him... and, just to survive!<br><br>The banter between Peter and Austin is hysterical... real laugh out loud funny! Peter keeps trying to push Austin away at every opportunity, emotionally distancing himself, but even open hostility is no deterrent for Austin.... He WANTS Peter. His body knows it and now even his mind is embracing it. YES!... he IS gay!<br><br>The relationship between Austin and Peter is a slow burner... with all the baggage Peter carries, he is stoically guarding himself from pain and any attraction... with his first responsibility to Cai. He is attracted to Austin but uses sex to avoid any emotional issues, where Austin just uses his humour to deflect his fixation for the object of his devotion... Peter! Austin also has to deal with issues from his past, his father is a complete bastard and bigot as was his Grandfather, his mother is AWOL in Europe and has been for years and he is supposed to be getting married in 8 weeks!... oh, and to top it all off he also has a commitment phobia! <br><br>Where Austin's life is an open book for all the world to see, and he is quite happy to let them, Peters life is hidden beneath complex layers. These layers are slowly peeled away, cleverly only allowing us to see glimpses of the man beneath and the turbulent and traumatic journey that brought him and his brothers into to Austin's world and the holy mess they now find themselves in. Peter might be a whore with steely resolve, but tiny sparks of emotion peak out of the cracks and give Austin hope... as he also sees the compassionate and strong man who cares for his brother... the man with a good heart!<br><br>This book is not all fun and games with Austin and Peter, they find themselves caught up in the investigation, there is murder, drugs and a plethora of other vices turning all their lives upside down. There are a whole host of characters in this book all of them well developed and smoothly integrated in to the tale. <br><br>Peters brother Cai is such a great character, I believe he deserves a mention... especially when the next book is focusing on him. He has a very damaged past and suffers with his bipolar, however the beauty and innocence of his heart glare at you through the pages, he is just so cute and expressive only wanting to please and I just wanted to delve in there and give him a hug!<br><br>Thank you, Thank you, Thank you Dani Alexander for letting us enjoy this novel through the eyes of Austin Glass... being in his mind with all of his inner musings, turmoil's, confusions and epiphanies was a joy. I am sure I now have permanent wrinkles from the constant grin on my face throughout this book. I was as captivated and enthralled by him... as he was with Bunny Slippers!<br><br>This is an excellent book... please do not wait to read it as I did! It is a true gem... read it now!<br><br><br><i>For more reviews, please visit...</i><a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/2012/11/shattered-glass-shattered-glass-1.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12863010271249299225" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1721696583" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1721696583" />
    <a title="James" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7365405-james"><img alt="James" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1522094190p2/7365405.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1721696583?book_show_action=true">Aug 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="James" class="user" itemprop="url" name="James" href="/user/show/7365405-james">James</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13504402-shattered-glass">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7365405-james?shelf=1-fiction">1-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7365405-james?shelf=7-arc-giveaway-won">7-arc-giveaway-won</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7365405-james?shelf=2-fic-other">2-fic-other</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1721696583" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6382347444415179513">After starting the Reading Challenge, I filled my "To Read" list with tons of crime thrillers, cozy mysteries and historical fiction novels. I've switched back and forth between the cozy and the grisly murders to my fascination with history and the complexities of family dramas... after 20 novels, I found myself wanting something different. I'm not one to read romance stories though I do enjoy quintessential "chick flick" films... either way, I stumbled upon <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13420351.Shattered_Glass__Shattered_Glass___1_' title='Shattered Glass (Shattered Glass, #1) by Dani Alexander' rel='nofollow noopener'>Shattered Glass</a> mostly because that w</span>
  <span id="freeText6382347444415179513" style="display:none">After starting the Reading Challenge, I filled my "To Read" list with tons of crime thrillers, cozy mysteries and historical fiction novels. I've switched back and forth between the cozy and the grisly murders to my fascination with history and the complexities of family dramas... after 20 novels, I found myself wanting something different. I'm not one to read romance stories though I do enjoy quintessential "chick flick" films... either way, I stumbled upon <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13420351.Shattered_Glass__Shattered_Glass___1_" title="Shattered Glass (Shattered Glass, #1) by Dani Alexander" rel="nofollow noopener">Shattered Glass</a> mostly because that was a title I was considering for a family drama in which I had started the outline [now I think I'll call it "Watching a Glass Shatter." I digress... back to Dani Alexander's "Shattered Glass."<br /><br />After reading some reviews and the love affair with bunny slippers (don't ask, you have to read it to understand), I thought to myself "this one may have potential" and ordered it online. When it arrived, I was just finishing the new Harry Potter book (talk about a vastly different world) but got to it the next day. It's about 350 pages long, so I expected about 5 to 6 hours of a read for me, so probably 5 days given that I have about an hour a day where I have time to read. Perhaps because it was a weekend, or maybe I chose to make more time because of how engaging it was, it only took me 2 days.<br /><br />Mind you, I have nothing to compare it to when it comes to either romance or gay fiction, having read very little of either, yet it feels like it's at the top of its category. It had mystery and intrigue, crime and thrills, some romance (well, mostly sex) and very bold characters that bordered on obnoxius and charming all at the same time (in a good way). I could never be best friends with either of the main characters as they would eventually annoy the hell out of me, but anyone would be blessed to have a friendship with either Austin or Peter given their intensity and committment to learning about each other.<br /><br />Could something like this ever really happen? Seems far-fetched, but I could be naive on the subject. Would someone really give up their entire career given the risks being taken? I suppose if they wanted to get out of their job, yes, but Austin seemed to love his job. It is fiction though, so I hold my disbelief given the amazing characters that are created and the sarcastic but real dialogue contained throughout the whole story.<br /><br />If you're looking for something with some spice, intrigue, passion and witty humor, definitely give it a read. If you are a bit faint of heart when it comes to this kinda stuff, it may be too much for a first read! I'll definitely read the second book in the series and will probably add it to the lineup for later this year after an Agatha Christie story and a cozy about a librarian who solves crimes.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <u>About Me</u>
  </i>
</b><br />For those new to me or my reviews... here's the scoop: I read A LOT. I write A LOT. And now I blog A LOT. First the book review goes on Goodreads, and then I send it on over to my WordPress blog at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://thisismytruthnow.com">https://thisismytruthnow.com</a>, where you'll also find TV &amp; Film reviews, the revealing and introspective 365 Daily Challenge and lots of blogging about places I've visited all over the world. And you can find all my social media profiles to get the details on the who/what/when/where and my pictures. Leave a comment and let me know what you think. Vote in the poll and ratings. Thanks for stopping by. <i>Note</i>: All written content is my original creation and copyrighted to me, but the graphics and images were linked from other sites and belong to them. Many thanks to their original creators.</span>

He is a trust fund baby, who has no relationship with his parents. <br/>While working on a case, Austin stumbles into a diner to meet an informant. Then he sees him. Bunny Slippers. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/f8cbdf04-e711-4c03-9b22-aca421466b07_zpsb0f46324.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408469i/799075.jpg' alt=' photo f8cbdf04-e711-4c03-9b22-aca421466b07_zpsb0f46324.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Bunny sli</span>
  <span id="freeText605605929244548580" style="display:none"><b>5 Fantastic and Funny Stars!!!!! </b><br><br>Before I go on and on about how much I <u>loved</u> this book, let me introduce you to these two guys...<br><br><b>DETECTIVE AUSTIN GLASS</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/206455a4-d757-4d0e-ab68-1ac05b6b80dc_zps0bf0f744.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794954i/598945.jpg" alt=" photo 206455a4-d757-4d0e-ab68-1ac05b6b80dc_zps0bf0f744.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/6f61b7ff-c755-496d-a152-d6667e3f8365_zps1f054a83.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408469i/799072.jpg" alt=" photo 6f61b7ff-c755-496d-a152-d6667e3f8365_zps1f054a83.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>AND<br><br>  <b>PETER ‘RABBIT’</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/88b96f94-83b5-48f2-a1eb-6bc7851a72ae_zps8ed8150d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408469i/799073.jpg" alt=" photo 88b96f94-83b5-48f2-a1eb-6bc7851a72ae_zps8ed8150d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/4b3971a7-b8dc-4ec5-9ed2-7b4e2bf97884_zps2abfdb33.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408469i/799074.jpg" alt=" photo 4b3971a7-b8dc-4ec5-9ed2-7b4e2bf97884_zps2abfdb33.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Austin is a twenty six year old detective, he is engaged to the beautiful Angelica, and on track to becoming an FBI agent. He is a trust fund baby, who has no relationship with his parents. <br>While working on a case, Austin stumbles into a diner to meet an informant. Then he sees him. Bunny Slippers. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/f8cbdf04-e711-4c03-9b22-aca421466b07_zpsb0f46324.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408469i/799075.jpg" alt=" photo f8cbdf04-e711-4c03-9b22-aca421466b07_zpsb0f46324.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Bunny slippers has red hair, blue eyes, and Austin is completely enamored with him. He can’t get this guy out of his head. It questions everything he’s ever thought about himself... Why am I attracted to this man? I like women.. WTF... The hilarious Austin even makes a list of reasons why he cannot be gay. It must just be bunny slippers...<br><b>
  <i> There was no way gay men watched as much ESPN as I did- another check to the ‘not gay’ column.</i>
</b><br><br>After days pass, he still can’t stop thinking about him. He can’t explain it, so he decides to confront the guy... It doesn’t go over too well...<br><b>
  <i>“I’m not gay.”<br>“Congratulations. Would you like a medal?” “I already have a medal. For bravery, not for being gay. I think you made me gay.” “I made you gay? Is that better or worse than the person who made you stupid?”</i>
</b><br><br>Eventually, Austin comes to terms with his sexuality. But how will it ever work with these two? Austin is a cop, Peter is into some questionable things... The case Austin is working on complicates things even more. Peter is involved to some extent. Their relationship is complicated to say the least. They can’t trust each other, but they have this connection, this chemistry that can’t be denied. Austin doesn’t want to feel the way he does for Peter, but he can’t stop it. <br><br> <a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/e0f7e701-a221-4bf0-82fe-7837430370d6_zps6ea04192.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408469i/799076.jpg" alt=" photo e0f7e701-a221-4bf0-82fe-7837430370d6_zps6ea04192.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book was perfect! I mean the perfect combination of action, suspense, love, sex, drama, and it was so funny, I couldn’t stand it!!! There is a lot going on in the plot- many twists and turns, things I didn’t see coming, which I am not going to go into as I feel that it would spoil the story- but there is some criminal activity, mystery, investigations etc. on top of Austin and Rabbit’s story. <br><br>Austin is my favorite type of character. Sarcastic, a bit arrogant, can be an asshole but is also sweet, sexy and funny as hell! It’s been a while since a character has made me laugh as much as this guy did! I absolutely adored him from the start! Peter took me a while to warm up to, at the beginning of the book- I wasn’t sure how I felt about him, but I ended up loving him too. Peter is a complex character, he has a crazy past, but he is a loving and completely devoted big brother, and even though he is only twenty- he is so much older at heart. <br><br>I am KICKING MYSELF for waiting as long as I did to read this one! I couldn’t put it down. Such a wonderful story. I laughed throughout the entire book and highlighted over 100 lines, but it was emotional for me too... There were several parts that had me in tears. The writing was excellent, the characters were fabulous- and not just the MC’s- I loved Austin’s parter Luis, and Darryl and Cai. I can’t wait for more from this author! I’m sure the next book will be just as good (Cai and hopefully Riley?) <br><br>Some of my favorite <u>FUNNY</u> lines...<br><br><b>Fact: Wednesday is commonly referred to as “hump day”- a.k.a Austin’s favorite day. <br><br>“You’re rich, spoiled, and used to getting your way.”<br> “Not true. If I had my way you would have kissed me and ridden me like a cowboy while screaming ‘yee-haw.’”<br><br>“You want to have sex in a men’s bathroom?”<br> “Huh? You said... Wasn’t it a signal? You coming in here? I read online that gay men did that.” <br>“Yah, in the 1960’s, Austin. Or at a Republican National Convention. Not on the first date in the bathroom of a restaurant in this century.”<br><br>My ex-girlfriend was right- men do suck.<br><br>“Asshole,” I muttered.<br>“Was that a directive?”<br><br>“Sucking in bed is probably why he’s changing teams.”<br><br>“This relationship can only take one smart ass if its going to survive.”<br><br>“Do you know what I did to the last guy that called me Tinkerbelle?” “Slept with him?” Darryl was silent for a second. “After that.”</b>  <br><br>Other lines I just <u>LOVED</u><br><br><b>“I’m not jealous over a guy I met a week ago.” </b><i>Yes, I was. Fucking ridiculously jealous over a guy I met a fucking, lousy-ass, goddamn week ago. </i><br><br><b>“You have all the power, Austin.”<br> “Is that what you believe? Do you think I have any power when it comes to you?”<br><br>Maybe Peter was the answer. The problem and the answer. The answer without being a solution. <br><br>“No strings attached. Unless you want strings.”</b><br><br><b>“People aren’t always who they seem, Detective. Am I anything like you thought?” <br>“No,” I admitted. </b><i>You’re a million times better than I could have imagined. </i><br><br><b>“Rabbit’s the rock we cling to when we’re drowning. He needs a mountain to hold him up, not another storm that’ll wear away at him.”<br><br>“Be selfish, Austin. Thats the only begging I can do. Be selfish.”</b>  <br><br>And my most favorite line of the whole book....<br><b>
  <i> “Tell me something good about your life,” <br><u>“You.”</u></i>
</b><br><br>I will leave you with one more thing.........<br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/SinsandNeedles-readnow.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222758i/649194.gif" alt=" photo SinsandNeedles-readnow.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_517343136" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/517343136" />
    <a title="Kat" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4878104-kat"><img alt="Kat" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515345527p2/4878104.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/517343136?book_show_action=true">Jan 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat" href="/user/show/4878104-kat">Kat</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781470005863" href="/book/show/13598341-shattered-glass">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=amusing-or-hilarious">amusing-or-hilarious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=first-time-gay">first-time-gay</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=nerdtastic">nerdtastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=mystery-suspense">mystery-suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer517343136" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10660823225687167084">Is this a conspiracy or mere coincidence? I can just SMELL a conspiracy...<br/><br/>I wasted so much money on crappy books, only to find that the truly incredible ones are either free - <i>The Administration</i> (wtf!), <i>Captive Prince</i> (wtf!), I'm sure there are more examples, still a bit green when it comes to m/m, but working on that! - ..Right. They're either free or... $ 2,99.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406797i/794074.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Hell! The chapter titles in <i>Shattered Glass</i> alone are worth more than $ 2,99! <br/><br/>This book was a complete surprise! As cheesy as the model</span>
  <span id="freeText10660823225687167084" style="display:none">Is this a conspiracy or mere coincidence? I can just SMELL a conspiracy...<br><br>I wasted so much money on crappy books, only to find that the truly incredible ones are either free - <i>The Administration</i> (wtf!), <i>Captive Prince</i> (wtf!), I'm sure there are more examples, still a bit green when it comes to m/m, but working on that! - ..Right. They're either free or... $ 2,99.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406797i/794074.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Hell! The chapter titles in <i>Shattered Glass</i> alone are worth more than $ 2,99! <br><br>This book was a complete surprise! As cheesy as the models on the cover look, so extraordinary and brilliant is <i>Shattered Glass</i> itself. Alexander crams so much creativity, plot, sparkling dialogue, three dimensional characters and humor into 350 pages...I have 9 pages of highlighted sentences on my ereader: the book is one big one liner! (<i>My body refused to allow me a suave, steady hand for my first blow job, "Late night with Angelica?" "A male prostitute." "you should watch what you say. One day someone's going to take you seriously."</i>) I'm fairly certain that I never laughed so hard during a sex scene that managed to be dirty hot at the same time. And I haven't even mentioned those well-written tender moments yet. <br><br>Alexander truly nailed it.<br><br>In essence, this is a coming out story. But it only very subtly touches upon the angst and intolerance that can unfortunately accompany such a step. Instead Alexander takes you on a hilarious, entertaining trip during which the narrator, smart ass and trust fund baby Austin Glass, strives to <i>thoroughly embrace the gay</i>.<br><br>So this Austin Glass... he's 26, about to marry a beautiful woman, his ambitions as a Detective are paying off; a career at the FBI never seemed closer. Then a freckled and pierced redhead with a killer bod serves him in a diner and life sucker punches Austin in the gut and while its at it also royally fucks him over. The redhead becomes an obsession. Worse, it's a Peter. So he's a guy, yes. Which makes Austin...gay? His life spirals out of control rapidly: his marriage is suddenly a sham, his career on the rocks, his father - a public figure - hates "faggots" and the sexy Peter turns out to be damaged goods; a male whore and a suspect in a murder case. Austin has tinier problems as well: because how the hell does gay sex work? <br><br><i>I felt like James Bond or Maxwell Smart - Inspector Clouseau? - furtively glancing left and right before following Peter into the bathroom. "What are you doing?", he asked, briefly glancing at the hand I used to pull him into a stall. I raised my brows and tugged his belt loose once we were inside, door closed. "I thought it was obvious?"<br>"You want to have sex in a men's bathroom?"<br>"Huh? You said...Wasn't it a signal? Your coming in here? I read online that gay men did that."<br>"Yah, in the 1960's Austin. Or at a Republican National Convention. Not on the first date in the bathroom of a restaurant. In this century."</i><br><br>Recommending books is risky business. But <i>Shattered Glass</i> I wholeheartedly recommend. It's fun, fun, fun and <i>way too</i> cheap! I'm out of here, going to add hundreds of <i> Shattered Glass</i> quotes. Go get it!<br><br><b>
  <i>Now that I've read this book a 2nd time, I realize that there's far too much plot, especially towards the end too much is going on, while there's not nearly enough Austin/Peter bonding. Oh well, I still dig the humor and creativity.;)</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10660823225687167084" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="~✡~Dαni(ela) ♥ ♂♂ love &amp; semi-colons~✡~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7999417-d-ni-ela-love-semi-colons"><img alt="~✡~Dαni(ela) ♥ ♂♂ love &amp; semi-colons~✡~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1485131784p2/7999417.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1033837799?book_show_action=true">Aug 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~✡~Dαni(ela) ♥ ♂♂ love &amp; semi-colons~✡~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~✡~Dαni(ela) ♥ ♂♂ love &amp; semi-colons~✡~" href="/user/show/7999417-d-ni-ela-love-semi-colons">~✡~Dαni(ela) ♥ ♂♂ love &amp; semi-colons~✡~</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to ~✡~Dαni(ela) ♥ ♂♂ love &amp; semi-colons~✡~ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/11588440-amy">Amy</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7999417-d-ni-ela-love-semi-colons?shelf=angst-central">angst-central</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7999417-d-ni-ela-love-semi-colons?shelf=age-gap">age-gap</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7999417-d-ni-ela-love-semi-colons?shelf=pure-fuckery">pure-fuckery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7999417-d-ni-ela-love-semi-colons?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7999417-d-ni-ela-love-semi-colons?shelf=skulls-build-a-snowman-2014">skulls-build-a-snowman-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7999417-d-ni-ela-love-semi-colons?shelf=bisexual-ofy">bisexual-ofy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1033837799" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6732913268706414308"><b>~~BUDDY READ WITH MISH & CORY~~</b><br/><br/>I apologize in advance for what I know is a ranty review, not my usual style, but this is most definitely a case of <b>Everyone-Loved-It-But-Me</b>.<br/><br/>This book was SO. DAMN. LONG. <br/><br/>Nearly 400 pages of repetitive, tedious babble, as narrated by Austin Glass, who is either a sociopath or just a really big fucking asshole:<br/><blockquote>
<em>I didn’t mourn her loss; nor did I think about the fact that I had caused her death. I had more important things to do. I spent the night fighting with Peter</em></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText6732913268706414308" style="display:none"><b>~~BUDDY READ WITH MISH &amp; CORY~~</b><br><br>I apologize in advance for what I know is a ranty review, not my usual style, but this is most definitely a case of <b>Everyone-Loved-It-But-Me</b>.<br><br>This book was SO. DAMN. LONG. <br><br>Nearly 400 pages of repetitive, tedious babble, as narrated by Austin Glass, who is either a sociopath or just a really big fucking asshole:<br><blockquote>
<em>I didn’t mourn her loss; nor did I think about the fact that I had caused her death. I had more important things to do. I spent the night fighting with Peter over the remote control.</em> </blockquote><br>PRIORITIES<br><br>Austin is a selfish, spoiled, self-indulgent cheater. His “love” interest is Peter, whom Austin refers to as a “whore” throughout most of the book. <br><br>Mind you, Peter’s no gem: <br><blockquote>
  <em>I’ve sucked and fucked enough to figure out that one dick is just like another, one vagina isn’t any more special than another, and I’ve got more important things to do than looking for a new trick every night. </em>
</blockquote><br>WHO KNEW?<br><br>This book meandered and dragged. There were numerous typos and editing issues (e.g., quote above). <br><br>The romance, if you can call it that, took a backburner to the crime/mystery/drama/angst, whatever the fuck you want to call the plot that strained all credibility. <br><br>The, uh, sweetness about killed me:<br><blockquote>
<em>Peter and I had finally settled the monogamy argument. We didn’t choose it because of society; or because we needed to be faithful to prove anything. We chose to be monogamous because we didn’t want to worry about condoms and HIV. It was hedonistic, really. </em> </blockquote><br>YOU DON'T SAY?<br><br>The tone was full of snark and what I think was supposed to pass as humor. I just found it gauche and mean-spirited. <br><br>When the MCs are unlikeable and the plot is boring as fuck with an unbelievable Oh-I’m-actually-gay revelation, and brimming with overly involved mothers and too many secondary characters to shake a stick at, what’s left? <br><br>Yeah, not much. <br><br>Then there’s the little cliffy at the end, a perfect little set-up for book 2. That shit just gives me a headache. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411146336ra/11197792.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
